</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">A</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a7e4dc46f-9686-4a9d-8b9a-aa9ec699c22b"><p>非递归路由必须具有指定的退出接口，可从该接口到达目标网络。在本例中，2001:db8:10:12::/64 为目标网络，R2 将使用退出接口 S0/0/0 到达该网络。因此，静态路由将是 ipv6 路由 2001:db8:10:12::/64 S0/0/0。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">C</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ab340e6b0-849e-41d3-8dd8-f61d70af3a3b"><p>因为浮动静态路由并不能用作主路由，所以其配置所要求的管理距离比常用的默认值 1 要高。当设置的管理距离比当前路由协议的管理距离更高时，距离&nbsp;参数只允许在主路由发生故障时才使用该路由。其他形式的静态路由作为主路由时有特定用途。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477316"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body addf9b3ff-2e36-4452-b686-0866f531f7d2" style="width: 740px;"><p>默认情况下在网络间发送网络状态相关消息并不安全。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477314"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a47128102-3e3a-4b67-a602-e47aa04fed85" style="width: 740px;"><p>仅适用于简单拓扑。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">C</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ae8437ff8-86a5-4fcd-aa1a-d67874e1719a"><p>默认情况下，动态路由协议跨网络转发消息，而不验证流量的接收者或发起者。随着网络增大，静态路由的配置复杂性也随之提高。静态路由更适合较小的网络。网络拓扑更改或链路禁用后，静态路由也需要人工干预。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">A</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ab79fc107-4810-4f43-8c51-f38e22eb0aa7"><p>要中断一个 IOS 进程（例如&nbsp;ping&nbsp;或&nbsp;traceroute），用户可以输入 Ctrl-Shift-6 键组合。Tab 用于完成命令参数或变量的其余部分。要退出配置模式并进入特权模式，可以使用 Ctrl-Z 按键。CTRL-R 将会重新显示当前键入的行，这样便于用户按 Enter 并重新发出&nbsp;ping&nbsp;命令。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div><div><div class="baseMargin___BRmsh"><div class="ant-radio-group ant-radio-group-outline ant-radio-group-middle css-oghtht"><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476895"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">A.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a3e2103ea-13f7-4f82-951f-bfcdbb127e2d" style="width: 740px;"><p>分支机构路由器</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476894"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a33811a91-2ada-48e0-a2ae-aad0f204b6da" style="width: 740px;"><p>网络边缘路由器</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">D</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a5acbb4e2-a40b-4343-88b7-b65e216189af"><p>网络边缘路由器提供客户交互性、个性化和移动性。只要客户具有互联网连接，就可以访问他们的内容。分支机构路由器提供简单的网络配置和管理，同时保持高度可用的网络。模块化路由器对于在网络设计和安装期间使用哪个接口提供更大的灵活性。运营商路由器提供端到端的可扩展解决方案。客户不会远程访问或直接连接到运营商路由器。</p>

<div class="questionItem___q6Hgu" id="Anchor_0_35"><div style="display: flex; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 40px; user-select: none;"><span class="questionScore___RW5tm mr10">2.0分</span><span class="font16 noWrap___X6AS3">36、</span><div class="  markdown-body a6fa98879-0277-4d09-a69d-4f0abc7b0ecb"><p>下列哪一项描述了采用默认硬件配置的 Cisco 1941 路由器的硬件特性？</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div><div><div class="baseMargin___BRmsh"><div class="ant-radio-group ant-radio-group-outline ant-radio-group-middle css-oghtht"><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476867"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">A.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a2cf944db-664a-4fa5-84b7-a9eb6e8f4090" style="width: 740px;"><p>它拥有三个用于 LAN 接入的 FastEthernet 接口。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476869"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">B.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a69139f7e-37e1-4492-b188-d9a7dbcbfbdc" style="width: 740px;"><p>它不需要 CPU，因为它依靠 Compact Flash 来运行 IOS。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476868"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a0e7d8e76-542c-4b4c-ba87-6055ce0a7f99" style="width: 740px;"><p>它提供两种类型的可用于访问控制台的端口。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476866"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a115ed295-4490-4899-82a4-c7022b8913ce" style="width: 740px;"><p>它没有 AUX 端口。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">C</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a7e99facd-7a16-4dbd-8f06-e0d8bf37007b"><p>Cisco 1941 路由器中的连接包括两种类型的端口用于初始配置和命令行界面管理访问。 这两种端口是常规 RJ-45 端口和新型 USB Type-B (mini-B USB) 连接器。 此外，该路由器具有一个用于远程管理访问的 AUX 端口和两个用于 LAN 访问的千兆以太网接口。 Compact Flash 可用于增加设备存储空间，但它不执行设备运行所需的 CPU 的功能。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div></div>
<div class="questionItem___q6Hgu" id="Anchor_0_36"><div style="display: flex; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 40px; user-select: none;"><span class="questionScore___RW5tm mr10">2.0分</span><span class="font16 noWrap___X6AS3">37、</span><div class="  markdown-body adf568654-2e4c-4acb-87d6-b33a98ff2c65"><p>请参见图示。在 192.168.0.32 网络中，路由器 R1 与路由器 ISP 属于 OSPF 邻居关系。当 OSPF 链路断开时，192.168.0.36 网络链路应作为备用链路。浮动静态路由命令 ip route 0.0.0.0 0.0.0.0 S0/0/1 100 已在 R1 上发出，即使 OSPF 链路已启用并且运转正常，当前流量依然使用备用链路。为了在启动时仅使用 OSPF 链路，应该如何更改静态路由命令？<img src="https://data.educoder.net/api/attachments/5830489" alt=","></p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div><div><div class="baseMargin___BRmsh"><div class="ant-radio-group ant-radio-group-outline ant-radio-group-middle css-oghtht"><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477211"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">A.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ad00984ad-0398-4c40-b8d0-4301681b6260" style="width: 740px;"><p>将管理距离更改为 1。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477213"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">B.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ac8d988f5-9f1a-469a-b9e9-cd489a797c16" style="width: 740px;"><p>将管理距离更改为 120。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477212"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a6bdb6d88-0a9f-4002-9163-dd068d7e7999" style="width: 740px;"><p>将目的网络更改为 192.168.0.34。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477210"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a084746d1-ffe6-4f94-b4a7-439b59adabbb" style="width: 740px;"><p>添加下一跳邻居地址 192.168.0.36。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">B</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a76fb2f1d-a172-4aa4-8220-8bda1d413a04"><p>当前浮动静态路由的问题是管理距离设置太低。管理距离需要高于 OSPF 的管理距离 110，以便路由器在启动时只使用 OSPF 链路。</p>

<div class="questionItem___q6Hgu" id="Anchor_0_37"><div style="display: flex; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 40px; user-select: none;"><span class="questionScore___RW5tm mr10">2.0分</span><span class="font16 noWrap___X6AS3">38、</span><div class="  markdown-body aaf31c48a-a9b9-4376-a2a9-7c1c7eb15127"><p>在路由器上配置的哪种类型的静态路由仅使用送出接口？</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">A</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body abadbf554-789e-4c65-b105-3b719fa710e4"><p>如果仅使用送出接口，则该路由是直连静态路由。如果使用下一跳 IP 地址，则该路由是递归静态路由。如果同时使用两个，则是完全指定静态路由。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div><div><div class="baseMargin___BRmsh"><div class="ant-radio-group ant-radio-group-outline ant-radio-group-middle css-oghtht"><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476899"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">A.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a42848f2e-0251-473d-b26e-af1efba3c4c5" style="width: 740px;"><p>模块化路由器</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476901"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">B.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a06fe5996-e46c-407b-bd71-0fc8d0c0b3a1" style="width: 740px;"><p>另一个非模块化配置路由器</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476900"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a85d745c1-787f-4e56-9812-09c9eb40baaf" style="width: 740px;"><p>PoE 设备</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476898"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a75940a5e-5833-4160-a315-4879268f798f" style="width: 740px;"><p>第 3 层交换机</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">A</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ad57a9d88-69d7-4d51-a080-add8c2d90c4c"><p>模块化路由器提供多个插槽，允许网络设计师更改或增加路由器上存在的接口。第 3 层交换机可以增加路由器上可用的端口数，但不会提供 WAN 连接。设备的 PoE 功能与它所拥有的端口数量无关。使用另一个非模块化配置路由器不会提供使用模块化路由器所能提供的灵活性，来适应未来增长。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">B</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a9545396e-3dfa-4ca4-b2ff-563d13e452a0"><p>带内设备管理通过网络连接来监控网络设备以及更改设备配置。使用带内管理执行配置时需要设备上至少有一个网络接口正常连接并运行，并且需要使用 Telnet、SSH 或 HTTP 访问设备。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477163"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">B.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a6b8c19bb-860c-4019-8fee-6c9529349aaf" style="width: 740px;"><p>192.168.10.0/24 网络的 EIGRP 学习的路由</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477162"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a4f0d8bd5-2359-45f0-a328-aa3a9cb7ac4b" style="width: 740px;"><p>192.168.10.0/24 网络的 OSPF 学习的路由</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477160"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body aa6c91159-767b-44a5-8446-62cd0daa56dd" style="width: 740px;"><p>默认路由</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">A</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body acf628d49-030d-4133-a0b5-2ed3a5fc1802"><p>若在静态路由端添加管理距离 5，则会为关闭的静态路由创造出一种浮动静态情况。静态路由具有的默认管理距离为 1。管理距离为 5 的该路由不会被置于路由表中，除非先前输入的 192.168.10.0/24 静态路由关闭或从未输入。若在静态路由配置端添加管理距离 5，则会创建浮动静态路由，该路由在同一目标网络的主路由关闭时将置于路由表中。默认情况下，192.168.10.0/24 网络的静态路由具有的管理距离为 1。因此，管理距离为 5 的浮动路由不会被置于路由表中，除非先前输入的 192.168.10.0/24 静态路由关闭或从未输入。由于浮动路由具有的管理距离为 5，所以该路由倾向于为同一目标网络的 OSPF 学习到的路由（管理距离为 110）或 EIGRP 学习到的路由（管理距离为 110）。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div></div>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div><div><div class="baseMargin___BRmsh"><div class="ant-radio-group ant-radio-group-outline ant-radio-group-middle css-oghtht"><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476734"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">A.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a24f4f3d7-66dc-4668-9b27-6b356ce5d39b" style="width: 740px;"><p>环回接口是路由器内部的逻辑接口。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476736"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">B.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ab34aaeaa-091b-4f23-9aa6-b261cedce123" style="width: 740px;"><p>将其分配给物流端口，并可将其连接至其他设备。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476735"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a3406cb30-be6c-4c59-b568-f02ed36b67d4" style="width: 740px;"><p>在路由器上仅可启用一个环回接口。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6476733"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a2abd1233-1dc4-4026-9c5c-e4125e2c28f4" style="width: 740px;"><p>要将该接口置于活动状态，需使用 no shutdown 命令。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">A</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a46e8e66b-8199-4e7d-962f-58037dbe0f99"><p>环回接口为内置于路由器的逻辑接口，且只要路由器运行正常，该接口就会自动处于活动状态。其并未分配到物理端口，因此从不会连接到其他任何设备。可以在一个路由器上启用多个环回接口。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">C</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body abfbf3ce8-c624-4b99-9c6a-9e3a874bfa8b"><p>浮动静态路由是管理距离超过已经在路由表中的另一路由的一个静态路由。如果表中的该路由消失，浮动静态路由将置于路由表中该路由的位置。内部 EIGRP 具有一个 90 的 AD，所以此场景中的浮动静态路由需要具有高于 90 的 AD。而且，在创建多接入接口的静态路由（类似 FastEthernet 分段）时，应该使用完全指定的路由，并且具有下一跳 IP 地址和退出接口。这可以防止路由器执行递归查询，但仍可确保多接入网段上的正确下一跳设备转发数据包。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">A</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body af26a2da4-4595-4a29-b1da-be09da643e8c"><p>将浮动静态路由用作备用路由，常常是从动态路由协议学习的路由。要成为浮动静态路由，配置的路由的管理距离必须超过主路由。例如，如果通过 OSPF 学习主路由，充当 OSPF 路由备用路由的浮动静态路由管理距离必须超过 110。浮动静态路由的管理距离置于静态路由结尾：ip route 209.165.200.228 255.255.255.248 10.0.0.1 120。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477195"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a11427c36-15cb-4ff1-891f-3cd1675140a0" style="width: 740px;"><p>验证 192.168.10.64 网络在网络基础设施内处于活动状态。</p>

<div class="questionItem___q6Hgu" id="Anchor_0_68"><div style="display: flex; align-items: baseline; margin-bottom: 40px; user-select: none;"><span class="questionScore___RW5tm mr10">2.0分</span><span class="font16 noWrap___X6AS3">69、</span><div class="  markdown-body a15e3b49e-1a85-4621-9dc9-f7a56bb78bcb"><p>与 IPv4 路由表条目相比，IPv6 路由表条目有什么不同之处？</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div><div><div class="baseMargin___BRmsh"><div class="ant-radio-group ant-radio-group-outline ant-radio-group-middle css-oghtht"><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477389"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">A.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a20c56848-bf6e-4ea7-a527-51878267a273" style="width: 740px;"><p>IPv6 是设计为无类的，因此所有路由实际上都是 1 级最终路由。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477391"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">B.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body aaf1424b6-7ed1-4f15-8564-78b372226176" style="width: 740px;"><p>IPv6 不使用静态路由填充路由表，而 IPv4 则使用静态路由。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477390"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ae6782f39-c4e3-489c-bf38-f64ce899c438" style="width: 740px;"><p>IPv6 路由是基于最短匹配前缀选择的，而 IPv4 路由是基于最长匹配前缀选择的。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-radio-wrapper ant-radio-wrapper-disabled noWrap___X6AS3 css-oghtht"><span class="ant-radio ant-radio-disabled"><input class="ant-radio-input" disabled="" type="radio" value="6477388"><span class="ant-radio-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body acaae6e5e-9ed1-478c-8283-77c9d9f41a96" style="width: 740px;"><p>IPv6 路由表包含 IPv4 路由表中没有的本地路由条目。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">A</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a75ddd4f9-b489-403e-84e0-98e84abfca53"><p>运行 IOS 15 版的路由器同时拥有 IPv4 和 IPv6 的本地链路路由表条目。IPv6 路由和 IPv4 路由的选用都是以最长匹配前缀为基础的。IPv6 和 IPv4 的路由表都会使用直连接口、静态路由和动态获取路由。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div></div>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">D</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ae012a99a-8d24-41b7-a828-6d40f87cb237"><p>不同的路由协议使用不同的度量来计算通过路由网络的最佳路径。RIP 使用跳数，EIGRP 使用带宽和延迟，以及 OSPF 使用开销。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">C</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a85c3d936-3483-4d33-a9ba-72f1c7dc7170"><p>IPv6 接口通常分配两个地址：本地链路地址和全局单播地址。本地链路地址的地址可能具有十六进制数字，第一个十六位元的范围是从 FE80 到 FEBF。全局单播数字的第一个十六位元中的前 3 位必须是 001。以 2001 开头的 IPv6 地址是全局单播地址的示例。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">D</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a7d348b1a-5c62-437f-be5b-f06a8e9b4a8f"><p>本地链路地址只与本地链路相关。路由器不会转发将本地链路地址用作源地址或目的地址的数据包。
IPv6 环回地址为 ::1/128。
唯一本地地址类似于 IPv4 私有地址。IPv6 协议中没有广播地址。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-checkbox-wrapper ant-checkbox-wrapper-disabled css-oghtht"><span class="ant-checkbox css-oghtht ant-checkbox-disabled"><input class="ant-checkbox-input" disabled="" type="checkbox" value="6477458"><span class="ant-checkbox-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a02210e29-0f9b-4385-9777-701dda6f1bb7"><p>是有类网络条目</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">AC</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a85a0db14-2022-4831-9d25-1fe139b13ed7"><p>最终路由是包含下一跳 IP 地址（另一路径）和/或退出接口的路由表条目。这意味着直连路由和本地链路路由都是最终路由。默认路由是第 1 级最终路由，但是并非所有最终路由都是默认路由。设为子网的路由表条目是第 1 级父路由，但是不满足成为最终路由的两项要求中的任一要求。最终路由不必是分类网络条目。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-checkbox-wrapper ant-checkbox-wrapper-disabled css-oghtht"><span class="ant-checkbox css-oghtht ant-checkbox-disabled"><input class="ant-checkbox-input" disabled="" type="checkbox" value="6476991"><span class="ant-checkbox-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">B.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a2ecf06cf-2c4d-418a-846b-a93dd35c8069"><p>闪存是非易失性存储器，包含 IOS 的有限部分。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-checkbox-wrapper ant-checkbox-wrapper-disabled css-oghtht"><span class="ant-checkbox css-oghtht ant-checkbox-disabled"><input class="ant-checkbox-input" disabled="" type="checkbox" value="6476994"><span class="ant-checkbox-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">C.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body acb3c2555-d9b6-4054-9d2f-3e8eb203eb30"><p>ROM 是非易失性存储器，包含基本诊断软件。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-checkbox-wrapper ant-checkbox-wrapper-disabled css-oghtht"><span class="ant-checkbox css-oghtht ant-checkbox-disabled"><input class="ant-checkbox-input" disabled="" type="checkbox" value="6476993"><span class="ant-checkbox-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">D.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ab6e81342-1f19-42ac-8690-4a093f9647d1"><p>NVRAM 是非易失性存储器，存储 IOS 的完整版本。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">AC</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a0e9ad5e2-f967-4ee4-91f9-ebc4fb97a4ab"><p>ROM 是非易失性存储器，存储启动说明、基本诊断软件和受限 IOS。闪存是非易失性存储器，用作 IOS 和其他相关系统文件的永久性存储。 RAM 是易失性存储器，存储 IP 路由表、ARP 缓存中 IPv4 到 MAC 地址的映射、缓冲或临时存储的数据包、运行配置以及当前运行的 IOS。 NVRAM 是非易失性存储器，存储启动配置文件。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">BE</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a11f16558-cf1e-426c-9ab7-08c2f1820077"><p>在路由器上已手动配置静态路由。静态路由不会自动更新，如果网络拓扑改变，必须手动重新配置静态路由。这样，静态路由就可以改善网络安全性，因为不在邻近路由器之间进行路由更新。静态路由还使用更少的带宽来提高资源效率，不使用 CPU 周期来计算并传播路由。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">AB</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a3168c3c7-08b7-4f2d-8a94-d0da0f318002"><p>路由器包含四种类型的存储器：</p>
<p>RAM - 易失存储器，用于存储运行 IOS、运行配置文件、路由表、ARP 表，并作为数据包缓冲器
ROM - 非易失存储器，用于保存有限版本的 IOS、启动指令和基本诊断软件
NVRAM - 非易失存储器，用于保存启动配置文件
Flash - 非易失存储器，用于保存 IOS 和其他系统文件</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-checkbox-wrapper ant-checkbox-wrapper-disabled css-oghtht"><span class="ant-checkbox css-oghtht ant-checkbox-disabled"><input class="ant-checkbox-input" disabled="" type="checkbox" value="6476975"><span class="ant-checkbox-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">E.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body ac997f74f-405b-4650-a2ce-1b84a6d6a012"><p>RAM 提供非易失性存储。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">AB</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a5af6b78c-f91e-4ec6-a10c-59f22f013ee0"><p>RAM 中会存储由设备用于支持网络运营的数据。 正在运行的配置文件存储在 RAM 中。 这种类型的内存被视为易失性存储器，因为重新启动时数据会丢失。 当设备启动时，闪存会存储 IOS 并将 IOS 副本传输到 RAM 中。 闪存是非易失性的，因为断电时它可以保留已存储的内容。</p>

</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div><div class="answerWrap___G9dnn"><label class="ant-checkbox-wrapper ant-checkbox-wrapper-disabled css-oghtht"><span class="ant-checkbox css-oghtht ant-checkbox-disabled"><input class="ant-checkbox-input" disabled="" type="checkbox" value="6477246"><span class="ant-checkbox-inner"></span></span><span><span class="font16 mr3" style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">E.</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a31789da3-2743-4832-ac1f-aeb0bb1be467"><p>由于静态路由不通过网络进行通告，因此比较安全。</p>
</div><div class="undefined hide"><div class="close___LKoWu"><span><i class="icon-quxiaozhiding"></i></span><span class=""><i class="icon-guanbi1"></i></span></div><div class="undefined undefined monaco___VnZC3 hide"></div></div></span></label></div></div></div><div class="analysisWrap___JoCnb"><div class="greyBg___vgesc"><div class="ant-row mb20 css-oghtht"><div class="ant-col font14 mr10 css-oghtht" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【答案】</div><div class="ant-col css-oghtht">DE</div></div><div class="ant-row css-oghtht"><span class="font14 mr10" style="color: rgb(106, 114, 131);">【解析】</span><div class="renderHtml___UerV1  markdown-body a0449d20b-5abf-4ed4-a56d-dc11d787e991"><p>静态路由需要充分了解整个网络才能正确实施。它非常容易出错，且不能针对大型网络扩展。静态路由使用更少的路由器资源，因为更新路由不需要计算。由于它不通过网络通告，静态路由也比较安全。</p>

(config)# ip route 192.168.10.0 255.255.255.0 95 
注意静态路由末尾的额外数字。只有当 EIGRP 获知的管理距离为 90 的路由中断时，路由表中才会显示该路由。当存在管理距离更好的路由时，路由表中不会出现该浮动静态路由。</p>
